        CASE WHEN ([Join1].[Id1] IS NULL) THEN CAST(NULL AS int) WHEN ([Join1].[Id2] IS NULL) THEN CAST(NULL AS int) WHEN ([Join1].[SeedTrayId] IS NULL) THEN 0 ELSE [Join1].[SeedTrayId] END AS [C1], 
        CASE WHEN ([Join1].[Id1] IS NULL) THEN CAST(NULL AS int) WHEN ([Join1].[Id2] IS NULL) THEN CAST(NULL AS int) ELSE 1 END AS [C2], 
        CASE WHEN ([Join1].[Id1] IS NULL) THEN CAST(NULL AS int) ELSE 1 END AS [C3]
        FROM   (SELECT [Project1].[Id] AS [Id], [Project1].[GenusId] AS [GenusId], [Project1].[SpecificName] AS [SpecificName], [Project1].[CommonName] AS [CommonName], [Project1].[Description] AS [Description], [Project1].[PropagationTime] AS [PropagationTime], [Project1].[Native] AS [Native]
            FROM ( SELECT

                [Extent1].[Native] AS [Native]

                WHERE (@p__linq__0 IS NULL OR [Extent1].[Native] = @p__linq__1) AND (@p__linq__2 IS NULL OR [Extent1].[SpecificName] = @p__linq__3)
            )  AS [Project1]
            ORDER BY row_number() OVER (ORDER BY [Project1].[GenusId] ASC)
            OFFSET 0 ROWS FETCH NEXT 20 ROWS ONLY  ) AS [Limit1]
        LEFT OUTER JOIN  (SELECT [Extent2].[Id] AS [Id1], [Extent2].[SpeciesId] AS [SpeciesId], [Extent2].[ProductTypeId] AS [ProductTypeId], [Extent2].[QuantityInStock] AS [QuantityInStock], [Extent3].[Id] AS [Id2], [Extent3].[PlantStockId] AS [PlantStockId], [Extent3].[Quantity] AS [Quantity], [Extent3].[JournalEntryTypeId] AS [JournalEntryTypeId], [Extent3].[TransactionDate] AS [TransactionDate], [Extent3].[Source] AS [Source], [Extent3].[SeedTrayId] AS [SeedTrayId], [Extent3].[Notes] AS [Notes]
            FROM  [dbo].[PlantStock] AS [Extent2]

    )  AS [Project2]

        [Join2].[Id3] AS [Id3], 
        [Join2].[PlantStockId] AS [PlantStockId], 
        [Join2].[Quantity] AS [Quantity], 
        [Join2].[JournalEntryTypeId] AS [JournalEntryTypeId], 
        [Join2].[TransactionDate] AS [TransactionDate], 
        [Join2].[Source] AS [Source], 
        [Join2].[Notes2] AS [Notes1], 
        CASE WHEN ([Join2].[Id1] IS NULL) THEN CAST(NULL AS int) WHEN ([Join2].[Id2] IS NULL) THEN CAST(NULL AS int) WHEN ([Join2].[Id3] IS NULL) THEN CAST(NULL AS int) WHEN ([Join2].[SeedTrayId] IS NULL) THEN 0 ELSE [Join2].[SeedTrayId] END AS [C1], 
        CASE WHEN ([Join2].[Id1] IS NULL) THEN CAST(NULL AS int) WHEN ([Join2].[Id2] IS NULL) THEN CAST(NULL AS int) WHEN ([Join2].[Id3] IS NULL) THEN CAST(NULL AS int) ELSE 1 END AS [C2], 
        CASE WHEN ([Join2].[Id1] IS NULL) THEN CAST(NULL AS int) WHEN ([Join2].[Id2] IS NULL) THEN CAST(NULL AS int) ELSE 1 END AS [C3], 
        CASE WHEN ([Join2].[Id1] IS NULL) THEN CAST(NULL AS int) ELSE 1 END AS [C4]
        FROM   (SELECT [Project1].[Id] AS [Id], [Project1].[GenusId] AS [GenusId], [Project1].[SpecificName] AS [SpecificName], [Project1].[CommonName] AS [CommonName], [Project1].[Description] AS [Description], [Project1].[PropagationTime] AS [PropagationTime], [Project1].[Native] AS [Native]
            FROM ( SELECT 
                [Extent1].[Id] AS [Id], 
                [Extent1].[GenusId] AS [GenusId], 
                [Extent1].[SpecificName] AS [SpecificName], 
                [Extent1].[CommonName] AS [CommonName], 
                [Extent1].[Description] AS [Description], 
                [Extent1].[PropagationTime] AS [PropagationTime], 
                [Extent1].[Native] AS [Native]
                FROM [dbo].[Species] AS [Extent1]
                WHERE (@p__linq__0 IS NULL OR [Extent1].[Native] = @p__linq__1) AND (@p__linq__2 IS NULL OR [Extent1].[SpecificName] = @p__linq__3)
            )  AS [Project1]
            ORDER BY row_number() OVER (ORDER BY [Project1].[Id] ASC)
            OFFSET 0 ROWS FETCH NEXT 20 ROWS ONLY  ) AS [Limit1]
        LEFT OUTER JOIN  (SELECT [Extent2].[Id] AS [Id1], [Extent2].[SpeciesId] AS [SpeciesId], [Extent2].[DateCollected] AS [DateCollected], [Extent2].[Location] AS [Location], [Extent2].[Notes] AS [Notes1], [Extent2].[SiteId] AS [SiteId], [Join1].[Id2], [Join1].[SeedBatchId], [Join1].[DatePlanted], [Join1].[Treatment], [Join1].[ThrownOut], [Join1].[Id3], [Join1].[PlantStockId], [Join1].[Quantity], [Join1].[JournalEntryTypeId], [Join1].[TransactionDate], [Join1].[Source], [Join1].[SeedTrayId], [Join1].[Notes2]
            FROM  [dbo].[SeedBatch] AS [Extent2]
            LEFT OUTER JOIN  (SELECT [Extent3].[Id] AS [Id2], [Extent3].[SeedBatchId] AS [SeedBatchId], [Extent3].[DatePlanted] AS [DatePlanted], [Extent3].[Treatment] AS [Treatment], [Extent3].[ThrownOut] AS [ThrownOut], [Extent4].[Id] AS [Id3], [Extent4].[PlantStockId] AS [PlantStockId], [Extent4].[Quantity] AS [Quantity], [Extent4].[JournalEntryTypeId] AS [JournalEntryTypeId], [Extent4].[TransactionDate] AS [TransactionDate], [Extent4].[Source] AS [Source], [Extent4].[SeedTrayId] AS [SeedTrayId], [Extent4].[Notes] AS [Notes2]
                FROM  [dbo].[SeedTray] AS [Extent3]
                LEFT OUTER JOIN [dbo].[JournalEntry] AS [Extent4] ON [Extent3].[Id] = [Extent4].[SeedTrayId] ) AS [Join1] ON [Extent2].[Id] = [Join1].[SeedBatchId] ) AS [Join2] ON [Limit1].[Id] = [Join2].[SpeciesId]
    )  AS [Project2]
    ORDER BY [Project2].[Id] ASC, [Project2].[C4] ASC, [Project2].[Id1] ASC, [Project2].[C3] ASC, [Project2].[Id2] ASC, [Project2].[C2] ASC
